Running.txt, notes in detail for building Stardict-tools (not needed anymore)

E. PARSING THE ENTRIES AND CREATING STARDICT FILES

The Ubuntu repo Stardict package in 16.04 LTS doesn't work since it doesn't support multiple lines having the
same entry name.

Ubuntu 22.04 LTS has @20230218 a newer stardict and stardict-tools v. than SourceForge,
3.0.7+git20211225+dfsg-1. So there is no need to build it oneself anymore.

cf. https://stardict-4.sourceforge.net/ChangeLog (link is in https://stardict-4.sourceforge.net/index_en.php)
  2022.
    StarDict-3.0.1.3 (Bodhisatta xxx) released.
    Support compress dictionary format!
    Some small changes!
  2022.
    StarDict-2.4.10 (Love-Cher xxx) released.
    Support compress dictionary format!
    Some small changes!
  2022.1.
    StarDict-3.0.7 (MasterWork xxx) released.
    Port to gtk3!
    Add some babylon dictionaries.
    Add some BigDict dictionaries.
    Add some PowerWord dictionaries.
    Stardict_client add md5 salt feature and RSA encrypt feature! As StarDict-Protocol_v04.
    Thanks Anatoly Sova <anatoliysova@gmail.com> for the bgl and dsl convert patch!
    Add fortune and cal plugins.
    Add info plugin.
    Add flite TTS plugin.
    Add YouDao.com netdict plugin.
    Thanks GreenLunar for the Hebrew translation!
    Many small changes.
  2022.1.
    StarDict-3.0.6.3 (Epic xxx) released.
    Provide Windows exe version.
    Source code is almost the same as StarDict-3.0.7!

dictzip
=======
In Ubuntu, install dictzip, which is used to produce the .dict.dz file:
sudo apt install dictzip

dictd
=====
Install dictd, if you want to lookup words from either Ubuntu supplied or self-built dictionary files locally.

Dictionary packages for dictd in Ubuntu
=======================================
Install any you want, e.g.

$ sudo apt install \
 dict-freedict-eng-fra \
 dict-freedict-lat-eng \
 dict-freedict-swe-deu \
 dict-freedict-swe-lat \
 dict-freedict-eng-spa \
 dict-freedict-swe-eng \
 dict-freedict-fin-nld \
 dict-freedict-ita-deu \
 dict-de-en

Building stardict-tools oneself (not recommended)
=================================================
Building 3.0.1 - not tried
--------------------------
Haven't tried building this in Ubuntu 22.04 LTS:

$ cd ~/Downloads/
$ wget https://stardict-4.sourceforge.net: https://sourceforge.net/projects/stardict-4/files/3.0.1/stardict-tools-3.0.1.tar.bz2/download -O stardict-tools-3.0.1.tar.bz2

Installing the whole 3.0.6.2 as a deb - fails, not needed
---------------------------------------------------------
$ cd ~/Downloads/
$ wget https://sourceforge.net/projects/stardict-4/files/3.0.6.2/stardict_3.0.6-2-1_all.deb/download -O stardict_3.0.6-2-1_all.deb 
$ dpkg -i stardict_3.0.6-2-1_all.deb

This didn't install in my Ubuntu 64b 16.04 LTS. It needs libsigc++-2.0-0c2a and I have libsigc++-2.0.0-v5.

Install libraries needed for building 3.0.6.2
---------------------------------------------
$ sudo apt install automake libtool gnome-common libglib2.0-dev libgtk2.0-dev libxml2-dev
$ sudo apt install libmysqlclient-dev libmysqlclient21 libgconf2-dev libgail-dev
$ sudo apt install gir1.2-gee-0.8 libgee-0.8-dev libglib2.0-doc

Building stardict-tools for 3.0.6.2
-----------------------------------
$ cd ~/Downloads/
$ wget https://sourceforge.net/projects/stardict-4/files/3.0.6.2/stardict-3.0.6.2-github-2.tar.xz/download -O stardict-3.0.6.2-github-2.tar.xz 
$ tar xfj stardict-3.0.6.tar.bz2
$ cd stardict-3.0.6/
$ ./autogen.sh
# This tells make we want to compile only the stardict-tools portion of the code
$ ./configure --disable-dict
$ make

Installing the deb for 3.0.6.3 - not tried?
-------------------------------------------
$ cd ~/Downloads/
$ wget https://sourceforge.net/projects/stardict-4/files/3.0.6.3/stardict_3.0.6.3-1_all.deb/download -O stardict_3.0.6.3-1_all.deb
$ sudo dpkg -i stardict_3.0.6.3-1_all.deb
???

Install libraries needed for building 3.0.6.3 - haven't managed to build this
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
$ sudo apt install p7zip-full
$ cd ~/Downloads/
# Download the sources
$ wget https://sourceforge.net/projects/stardict-4/files/3.0.6.3/stardict-3.0.6.3-2-src.7z/download -O stardict-3.0.6.3-2-src.7z
$ 7z x stardict-3.0.6.3-2-src.7z

sudo apt install automake libtool gnome-common gnome-devel

Building whole 3.0.6.3, gnome-doc-utils - fails and not needed
-------------------------------------------------------------- 
Besides the above libraries, build 3.0.6.3 seems to need at least "gnome-doc-utils".
It is however not present in newer Ubuntus such as 22.04 LTS.

Ubuntu 18.04 still had gnome-doc-utils. Installing it fails:

$ cd ~/Downloads/
# Link to the old gnome-doc-utils-deb is in https://ubuntu.pkgs.org/18.04/ubuntu-universe-amd64/gnome-doc-utils_0.20.10-4_all.deb.html
$ wget http://archive.ubuntu.com/ubuntu/pool/universe/g/gnome-doc-utils/gnome-doc-utils_0.20.10-4_all.deb -O gnome-doc-utils_0.20.10-4_all.deb
# Installing the deb won't work in 22.04 LTS:
$ sudo dpkg -i gnome-doc-utils_0.20.10-4_all.deb
  gnome-doc-utils (0.20.10-4) ...
  dpkg: dependency problems prevent configuration of gnome-doc-utils:
    gnome-doc-utils depends on python:any (<< 2.8).
    gnome-doc-utils depends on python:any (>= 2.7.5-5~).
    gnome-doc-utils depends on python-libxml2

In 22.04, python is forced to be python3. Installing python2.7 doesn't help. It doesn't really install python2.
A python3-libxml2 exists, but not python-libxml2.
